dimension\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDefine variables to hold the values for each dimension\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDo not use netCDF groups, unsigned 64-bit integers, or user-defined variable types, since these are not widely supported by generalized science software\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvide two global attributes \u003ccode\u003eData_Start\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eData_End\u003c/code\u003e with value = yyyy-mm-ddThh:mm:ss UTC\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eRecommend using the CDF_TIME_TT2000 variable type as 8-byte integers in netCDF, and using the CDF library routines for conversion to and from other time formats. Otherwise, time variables should be in seconds from some epoch, with \u003ccode\u003eUNITS\u003c/code\u003e of \"seconds since 2000-01-01\", for instance.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn addition to the ISTP-defined \u003ccode\u003eFILLVAL\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eCATDESC\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eUNITS\u003c/code\u003e, netCDF conventions call for also storing in \u003ccode\u003e_FillValue\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003elong_name\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003eunits\u003c/code\u003e, respectively. data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Best practices for creating a ISTP-compliant dataset in CDF and netCDF formats</h1><a id="user-content-best-practices-for-creating-a-istp-compliant-dataset-in-cdf-and-netcdf-formats" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Best practices for creating a ISTP-compliant dataset in CDF and netCDF formats" href="#best-practices-for-creating-a-istp-compliant-dataset-in-cdf-and-netcdf-formats"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dataset and filenaming recommmendations</h2><a id="user-content-dataset-and-filenaming-recommmendations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dataset and filenaming recommmendations" href="#dataset-and-filenaming-recommmendations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Follow the SPDF <a href="https://spdf.gsfc.nasa.gov/guidelines/filenaming_recommendations.html" rel="nofollow">Recommended File and Data Collection Naming Practices</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">note: perhaps move the above file into the ISTP Github and change SPDF pointer to it</h3><a id="user-content-note-perhaps-move-the-above-file-into-the-istp-github-and-change-spdf-pointer-to-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: note: perhaps move the above file into the ISTP Github and change SPDF pointer to it" href="#note-perhaps-move-the-above-file-into-the-istp-github-and-change-spdf-pointer-to-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CDF-specific practices</h2><a id="user-content-cdf-specific-practices" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CDF-specific practices" href="#cdf-specific-practices"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">netCDF-specific practices</h2><a id="user-content-netcdf-specific-practices" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: netCDF-specific practices" href="#netcdf-specific-practices"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use time as the unlimited dimension</li>
<li>Define variables to hold the values for each dimension</li>
<li>Do not use netCDF groups, unsigned 64-bit integers, or user-defined variable types, since these are not widely supported by generalized science software</li>
<li>Provide two global attributes <code>Data_Start</code> and <code>Data_End</code> with value = yyyy-mm-ddThh:mm:ss UTC</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Recommend using the CDF_TIME_TT2000 variable type as 8-byte integers in netCDF, and using the CDF library routines for conversion to and from other time formats. Otherwise, time variables should be in seconds from some epoch, with <code>UNITS</code> of "seconds since 2000-01-01", for instance.</p>
<p dir="auto">In addition to the ISTP-defined <code>FILLVAL</code>, <code>CATDESC</code> and <code>UNITS</code>, netCDF conventions call for also storing in <code>_FillValue</code>, <code>long_name</code>, and <code>units</code>, respectively.  See <a href="https://docs.unidata.ucar.edu/netcdf-c/4.9.2/attribute_conventions.html" rel="nofollow">netCDF Attribute Conventions</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tools for laying out the dataset</h2><a id="user-content-tools-for-laying-out-the-dataset" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tools for laying out the dataset" href="#tools-for-laying-out-the-dataset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Metadata editors</h2><a id="user-content-metadata-editors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Metadata editors" href="#metadata-editors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Browser--based <a href="https://spdf.gsfc.nasa.gov/istp-metadata-editor/" rel="nofollow">ISTP Metadata Editor</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://spdf.gsfc.nasa.gov/skteditor/" rel="nofollow">SKTEditor</a>, a Java downloadable program that aids the user with the creation of a Skeleton CDF.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding Data to Skeleton CDFs</h2><a id="user-content-adding-data-to-skeleton-cdfs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding Data to Skeleton CDFs" href="#adding-data-to-skeleton-cdfs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Use IDLmakecdf program</h3><a id="user-content-use-idlmakecdf-program" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Use IDLmakecdf program" href="#use-idlmakecdf-program"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">produces a CDF file using IDL with a Skeleton CDF file and user-supplied IDL code to read user data.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://spdf.gsfc.nasa.gov/CDAWlib.html" rel="nofollow">IDLmakecdf</a> (IDL software and on-line help)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Use makeCDF program</h3><a id="user-content-use-makecdf-program" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Use makeCDF program" href="#use-makecdf-program"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">produces a CDF file (using C) when given 3 input files: (1) data file, (2) translation file, (3) Skeleton CDF file.</p>

</ul>
